"main.py
```python
'''
Main application file for real-time object detection and tracking.
'''
import cv2
from gui import App
from detection import YOLOv8Detector
from tracking import Tracker
from utils import optimize_with_tensorrt
def initialize_camera():
    '''
    Initialize camera feed.
    '''
    cap = cv2.VideoCapture(0)  # Assuming the first camera device
    if not cap.isOpened():
        raise Exception("Error: Camera could not be initialized.")
    return cap
def initialize_yolo():
    '''
    Load YOLOv8 model.
    '''
    detector = YOLOv8Detector()
    return detector
def initialize_tracker():
    '''
    Initialize tracker.
    '''
    tracker = Tracker()
    return tracker
def process_frame(frame, detector, tracker):
    '''
    Detect objects and update tracker.
    '''
    detections = detector.detect_objects(frame)
    tracks = tracker.update_tracks(detections)
    return tracks
def main():
    '''
    Main function to run the application.
    '''
    try:
        # Initialize components
        cap = initialize_camera()
        detector = initialize_yolo()
        tracker = initialize_tracker()
        # Optimize models with TensorRT
        optimize_with_tensorrt(detector)
        # Initialize GUI
        app = App()
        while True:
            ret, frame = cap.read()
            if not ret:
                print("Error: Frame could not be read from camera.")
                break
            # Process frame
            tracks = process_frame(frame, detector, tracker)
            # Update GUI
            app.display_frame(frame)
            app.display_metadata(tracks)
            # Break on 'q' key press
            if cv2.waitKey(1) & 0xFF == ord('q'):
                break
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"An error occurred: {e}")
    finally:
        cap.release()
        cv2.destroyAllWindows()
if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```
gui.py
```python
'''
GUI module for displaying video feed and metadata.
'''
import cv2
from tkinter import Tk, Label
from PIL import Image, ImageTk
class App:
    def __init__(self):
        '''
        Initialize the GUI application.
        '''
        self.root = Tk()
        self.setup_ui()
    def setup_ui(self):
        '''
        Setup the user interface.
        '''
        self.root.title("Object Detection and Tracking")
        self.label = Label(self.root)
        self.label.pack()
    def display_frame(self, frame):
        '''
        Display the video frame in the GUI.
        '''
        frame_rgb = cv2.cvtColor(frame, cv2.COLOR_BGR2RGB)
        image = Image.fromarray(frame_rgb)
        photo = ImageTk.PhotoImage(image=image)
        self.label.config(image=photo)
        self.label.image = photo  # Keep a reference to avoid garbage collection
        self.root.update_idletasks()  # Update the GUI
    def display_metadata(self, tracks):
        '''
        Display metadata in the GUI.
        '''
        print("Tracks:", tracks)
    def run(self):
        '''
        Run the GUI application.
        '''
        self.root.mainloop()
```
detection.py
```python
'''
Detection module using YOLOv8.
'''
import torch
from ultralytics import YOLO
import numpy as np
import pycuda.driver as cuda
class YOLOv8Detector:
    def __init__(self, model_path='yolov8.pt'):
        '''
        Initialize YOLOv8 detector.
        '''
        self.model = YOLO(model_path)
        self.engine = None
        self.context = None
        self.d_input = None
        self.d_output = None
        self.input_shape = None
        self.output_shape = None
    def detect_objects(self, frame):
        '''
        Detect objects in the given frame.
        '''
        if self.engine is not None:
            frame_resized = cv2.resize(frame, (self.input_shape[2], self.input_shape[1]))
            frame_normalized = frame_resized.astype(np.float32) / 255.0
            frame_transposed = np.transpose(frame_normalized, (2, 0, 1)).ravel()
            cuda.memcpy_htod(self.d_input, frame_transposed)
            self.context.execute_v2(bindings=[int(self.d_input), int(self.d_output)])
            output = np.empty(self.output_shape, dtype=np.float32)
            cuda.memcpy_dtoh(output, self.d_output)
            detections = self.process_output(output)
        else:
            results = self.model(frame)
            detections = []
            for result in results.xyxy[0]:
                x1, y1, x2, y2, conf, cls = result
                detections.append({
                    'bbox': [x1.item(), y1.item(), x2.item(), y2.item()],
                    'confidence': conf.item(),
                    'class': int(cls.item())
                })
        return detections
    def process_output(self, output):
        '''
        Process the output from TensorRT inference.
        '''
        detections = []
        for det in output:
            x1, y1, x2, y2, conf, cls = det
            detections.append({
                'bbox': [x1, y1, x2, y2],
                'confidence': conf,
                'class': int(cls)
            })
        return detections
```
tracking.py
```python
'''
Tracking module using DeepSORT.
'''
from deep_sort.deep_sort import DeepSort
import numpy as np
class Tracker:
    def __init__(self):
        # Initialize DeepSORT tracker
        self.tracker = DeepSort(
            model_path='deep_sort_model.ckpt',  # Path to the DeepSORT model
            max_dist=0.2,
            min_confidence=0.3,
            nms_max_overlap=0.5,
            max_iou_distance=0.7,
            max_age=70,
            n_init=3,
            nn_budget=100
        )
    def update_tracks(self, detections):
        # Convert detections to the format required by DeepSORT
        bbox_xywh = np.array([det['bbox'] for det in detections])
        confidences = np.array([det['confidence'] for det in detections])
        classes = np.array([det['class'] for det in detections])
        # Update tracker with new detections
        tracks = self.tracker.update(bbox_xywh, confidences, classes)
        # Format tracks for output
        formatted_tracks = []
        for track in tracks:
            formatted_tracks.append({
                'track_id': track.track_id,
                'bbox': track.to_tlbr(),
                'class': track.cls,
                'confidence': track.confidence
            })
        return formatted_tracks
```
utils.py
```python
'''
Utility functions for optimization and other tasks.
'''
import tensorrt as trt
import pycuda.driver as cuda
import pycuda.autoinit
def optimize_with_tensorrt(detector):
    '''
    Optimize the YOLOv8 model with TensorRT.
    '''
    # Create a TensorRT logger
    logger = trt.Logger(trt.Logger.WARNING)
    # Create a builder and network
    builder = trt.Builder(logger)
    network = builder.create_network(1 << int(trt.NetworkDefinitionCreationFlag.EXPLICIT_BATCH))
    # Parse the ONNX model to TensorRT
    onnx_path = 'yolov8.onnx'  # Assuming the model is converted to ONNX format
    with trt.OnnxParser(network, logger) as parser:
        with open(onnx_path, 'rb') as model:
            if not parser.parse(model.read()):
                print('ERROR: Failed to parse the ONNX file.')
                for error in range(parser.num_errors):
                    print(parser.get_error(error))
                return
    # Build the engine
    builder.max_workspace_size = 1 << 30  # 1GB
    builder.max_batch_size = 1
    engine = builder.build_cuda_engine(network)
    # Allocate buffers for input and output
    input_shape = network.get_input(0).shape
    output_shape = network.get_output(0).shape
    input_size = trt.volume(input_shape) * trt.float32.itemsize
    output_size = trt.volume(output_shape) * trt.float32.itemsize
    d_input = cuda.mem_alloc(input_size)
    d_output = cuda.mem_alloc(output_size)
    # Create a context
    context = engine.create_execution_context()
    # Store the optimized engine and context in the detector
    detector.engine = engine
    detector.context = context
    detector.d_input = d_input
    detector.d_output = d_output
    detector.input_shape = input_shape
    detector.output_shape = output_shape
```

"main.py
```python
'''
Main application file for real-time object detection and tracking.
'''
import cv2
from gui import App
from detection import YOLOv8Detector
from tracking import Tracker
from utils import optimize_with_tensorrt
def initialize_camera():
    '''
    Initialize camera feed.
    '''
    cap = cv2.VideoCapture(0)  # Assuming the first camera device
    if not cap.isOpened():
        raise Exception("Error: Camera could not be initialized.")
    return cap
def initialize_yolo():
    '''
    Load YOLOv8 model.
    '''
    detector = YOLOv8Detector()
    return detector
def initialize_tracker():
    '''
    Initialize tracker.
    '''
    tracker = Tracker()
    return tracker
def process_frame(frame, detector, tracker):
    '''
    Detect objects and update tracker.
    '''
    detections = detector.detect_objects(frame)
    tracks = tracker.update_tracks(detections)
    return tracks
def main():
    '''
    Main function to run the application.
    '''
    try:
        # Initialize components
        cap = initialize_camera()
        detector = initialize_yolo()
        tracker = initialize_tracker()
        # Optimize models with TensorRT
        optimize_with_tensorrt(detector)
        # Initialize GUI
        app = App()
        while True:
            ret, frame = cap.read()
            if not ret:
                print("Error: Frame could not be read from camera.")
                break
            # Process frame
            tracks = process_frame(frame, detector, tracker)
            # Update GUI
            app.display_frame(frame)
            app.display_metadata(tracks)
            # Break on 'q' key press
            if cv2.waitKey(1) & 0xFF == ord('q'):
                break
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"An error occurred: {e}")
    finally:
        cap.release()
        cv2.destroyAllWindows()
if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

gui.py
```python
'''
GUI module for displaying video feed and metadata.
'''
import cv2
from tkinter import Tk, Label
from PIL import Image, ImageTk
class App:
    def __init__(self):
        '''
        Initialize the GUI application.
        '''
        self.root = Tk()
        self.setup_ui()
    def setup_ui(self):
        '''
        Setup the user interface.
        '''
        self.root.title("Object Detection and Tracking")
        self.label = Label(self.root)
        self.label.pack()
    def display_frame(self, frame):
        '''
        Display the video frame in the GUI.
        '''
        frame_rgb = cv2.cvtColor(frame, cv2.COLOR_BGR2RGB)
        image = Image.fromarray(frame_rgb)
        photo = ImageTk.PhotoImage(image=image)
        self.label.config(image=photo)
        self.label.image = photo  # Keep a reference to avoid garbage collection
        self.root.update_idletasks()  # Update the GUI
    def display_metadata(self, tracks):
        '''
        Display metadata in the GUI.
        '''
        print("Tracks:", tracks)
    def run(self):
        '''
        Run the GUI application.
        '''
        self.root.mainloop()
```

detection.py
```python
'''
Detection module using YOLOv8.
'''
import torch
from ultralytics import YOLO
import numpy as np
import pycuda.driver as cuda
class YOLOv8Detector:
    def __init__(self, model_path='yolov8.pt'):
        '''
        Initialize YOLOv8 detector.
        '''
        self.model = YOLO(model_path)
        self.engine = None
        self.context = None
        self.d_input = None
        self.d_output = None
        self.input_shape = None
        self.output_shape = None
    def detect_objects(self, frame):
        '''
        Detect objects in the given frame.
        '''
        if self.engine is not None:
            frame_resized = cv2.resize(frame, (self.input_shape[2], self.input_shape[1]))
            frame_normalized = frame_resized.astype(np.float32) / 255.0
            frame_transposed = np.transpose(frame_normalized, (2, 0, 1)).ravel()
            cuda.memcpy_htod(self.d_input, frame_transposed)
            self.context.execute_v2(bindings=[int(self.d_input), int(self.d_output)])
            output = np.empty(self.output_shape, dtype=np.float32)
            cuda.memcpy_dtoh(output, self.d_output)
            detections = self.process_output(output)
        else:
            results = self.model(frame)
            detections = []
            for result in results.xyxy[0]:
                x1, y1, x2, y2, conf, cls = result
                detections.append({
                    'bbox': [x1.item(), y1.item(), x2.item(), y2.item()],
                    'confidence': conf.item(),
                    'class': int(cls.item())
                })
        return detections
    def process_output(self, output):
        '''
        Process the output from TensorRT inference.
        '''
        detections = []
        for det in output:
            x1, y1, x2, y2, conf, cls = det
            detections.append({
                'bbox': [x1, y1, x2, y2],
                'confidence': conf,
                'class': int(cls)
            })
        return detections
```

tracking.py
```python
'''
Tracking module using DeepSORT.
'''
from deep_sort.deep_sort import DeepSort
import numpy as np
class Tracker:
    def __init__(self):
        # Initialize DeepSORT tracker
        self.tracker = DeepSort(
            model_path='deep_sort_model.ckpt',  # Path to the DeepSORT model
            max_dist=0.2,
            min_confidence=0.3,
            nms_max_overlap=0.5,
            max_iou_distance=0.7,
            max_age=70,
            n_init=3,
            nn_budget=100
        )
    def update_tracks(self, detections):
        # Convert detections to the format required by DeepSORT
        bbox_xywh = np.array([det['bbox'] for det in detections])
        confidences = np.array([det['confidence'] for det in detections])
        classes = np.array([det['class'] for det in detections])
        # Update tracker with new detections
        tracks = self.tracker.update(bbox_xywh, confidences, classes)
        # Format tracks for output
        formatted_tracks = []
        for track in tracks:
            formatted_tracks.append({
                'track_id': track.track_id,
                'bbox': track.to_tlbr(),
                'class': track.cls,
                'confidence': track.confidence
            })
        return formatted_tracks
```

utils.py
```python
'''
Utility functions for optimization and other tasks.
'''
import tensorrt as trt
import pycuda.driver as cuda
import pycuda.autoinit
def optimize_with_tensorrt(detector):
    '''
    Optimize the YOLOv8 model with TensorRT.
    '''
    # Create a TensorRT logger
    logger = trt.Logger(trt.Logger.WARNING)
    # Create a builder and network
    builder = trt.Builder(logger)
    network = builder.create_network(1 << int(trt.NetworkDefinitionCreationFlag.EXPLICIT_BATCH))
    # Parse the ONNX model to TensorRT
    onnx_path = 'yolov8.onnx'  # Assuming the model is converted to ONNX format
    with trt.OnnxParser(network, logger) as parser:
        with open(onnx_path, 'rb') as model:
            if not parser.parse(model.read()):
                print('ERROR: Failed to parse the ONNX file.')
                for error in range(parser.num_errors):
                    print(parser.get_error(error))
                return
    # Build the engine
    builder.max_workspace_size = 1 << 30  # 1GB
    builder.max_batch_size = 1
    engine = builder.build_cuda_engine(network)
    # Allocate buffers for input and output
    input_shape = network.get_input(0).shape
    output_shape = network.get_output(0).shape
    input_size = trt.volume(input_shape) * trt.float32.itemsize
    output_size = trt.volume(output_shape) * trt.float32.itemsize
    d_input = cuda.mem_alloc(input_size)
    d_output = cuda.mem_alloc(output_size)
    # Create a context
    context = engine.create_execution_context()
    # Store the optimized engine and context in the detector
    detector.engine = engine
    detector.context = context
    detector.d_input = d_input
    detector.d_output = d_output
    detector.input_shape = input_shape
    detector.output_shape = output_shape
```

```markdown
# Real-Time Object Detection and Tracking System for ISR Drone

This software enables real-time object detection and tracking for ISR drones using YOLOv8 for detection and DeepSORT for tracking. It is optimized for efficiency with TensorRT and integrates seamlessly with live camera feeds on NVIDIA Jetson Orin NX.

## 📖 Main Functions

### 1. Object Detection
The software utilizes YOLOv8 for detecting objects in real-time. It identifies objects and outputs their bounding boxes, confidence scores, and class labels.

### 2. Object Tracking
DeepSORT is used to track detected objects across frames, assigning unique IDs to each tracked object and maintaining their trajectories.

### 3. Real-Time Metadata Output
The system outputs metadata for detected and tracked objects, including bounding box coordinates, confidence scores, class labels, and tracking IDs.

### 4. Live Camera Feed Integration
The software integrates with live camera feeds, processing frames in real-time for detection and tracking.

### 5. TensorRT Optimization
The YOLOv8 model is optimized using TensorRT for efficient inference on NVIDIA Jetson Orin NX.

### 6. User-Friendly GUI
A graphical user interface (GUI) displays the live video feed and metadata for detected and tracked objects.

---

## 🚀 Quick Install

### Step 1: Clone the Repository
Clone the repository containing the software:
```bash
git clone https://github.com/your-repository/object-detection-tracking.git
cd object-detection-tracking
```

### Step 2: Install Dependencies
Install the required Python dependencies using `pip`:
```bash
pip install -r requirements.txt
```

### Step 3: Install TensorRT
Ensure TensorRT is installed on your NVIDIA Jetson Orin NX. Follow the official NVIDIA TensorRT installation guide: [TensorRT Installation Guide](https://docs.nvidia.com/deeplearning/tensorrt/install-guide/index.html).

### Step 4: Install DeepSORT Model
Download the DeepSORT model file (`deep_sort_model.ckpt`) and place it in the appropriate directory.

---

## 🛠️ How to Use

### Step 1: Prepare the Environment
Ensure your NVIDIA Jetson Orin NX is set up with the necessary drivers and libraries. Connect the camera to the device.

### Step 2: Run the Application
Execute the main application file:
```bash
python main.py
```

### Step 3: Interact with the GUI
- The GUI will display the live camera feed.
- Detected and tracked objects will be highlighted with bounding boxes.
- Metadata for each object will be displayed in the console.

### Step 4: Stop the Application
Press the `q` key to stop the application and close the GUI.

---

## 📋 Notes

### Supported Hardware
- NVIDIA Jetson Orin NX
- Camera compatible with OpenCV

### Supported Models
- YOLOv8 for object detection
- DeepSORT for object tracking

### File Structure
- `main.py`: Main application file.
- `gui.py`: GUI module for displaying video feed and metadata.
- `detection.py`: YOLOv8 detection module.
- `tracking.py`: DeepSORT tracking module.
- `utils.py`: Utility functions for TensorRT optimization.

---

## 🛡️ Troubleshooting

### Camera Initialization Error
If the camera fails to initialize, ensure it is properly connected and compatible with OpenCV.

### TensorRT Optimization Error
Ensure the YOLOv8 model is converted to ONNX format and TensorRT is correctly installed.

### GUI Display Issues
Ensure all GUI dependencies (`Pillow`, `Tkinter`) are installed.

---

## 📖 Documentation

For detailed documentation on YOLOv8, DeepSORT, and TensorRT, refer to:
- [YOLOv8 Documentation](https://docs.ultralytics.com)
- [DeepSORT Documentation](https://github.com/nwojke/deep_sort)
- [TensorRT Documentation](https://docs.nvidia.com/deeplearning/tensorrt)

---
